### [11:10→14:15 retrospective] — **RULE UPDATE: time-horizon discipline after LINK flip-flop**

Operator flagged LINK SHORT place+cancel (7-min lifecycle) as flip-flop. Diagnosis: invalidation threshold "BTC >75100" thinner than ATR(15m) ~280 pts. Horizon mismatch: 3m-noise cancel on 1H-structure thesis.

**Rules added (CLAUDE.md § Time-horizon discipline, lesson logged):**

1. Invalidation thresholds must exceed ATR(15m) OR pair with structural confirm. Single-price thresholds <0.5% forbidden.
2. Pending limits: 15-min grace period from placement. Only catastrophic events (BTC >1% move, high-impact news, broken structural level) bypass grace.
3. Re-score pending limits on 15m candle close, not every 3m /loop fire.
4. 45-min maxAge remains for routine expiration.

**Also:** Removed hardcoded limit-placed/cancelled TG boilerplate (src/executor.ts, src/execute.ts). Claude sends single human-language TG via send-tg.ts --file per new templates 2+6 in telegram-templates.md. Orchestrator-level TTL auto-cancel keeps its TG as fallback.

**Retroactive grade of LINK trade:** process B (pre-committed rule worked AS DESIGNED at time), but rule THRESHOLD was wrong. Counterfactual under new rules: grace period would hold limit к 11:15 (first 15m close after placement). At that close BTC was still ~75130; re-scoring at 15m close would evaluate full picture, not mid-bar spike.

### [17:43] — ⚠️ BTC LONG #3 CANCELLED — MARGIN RULE VIOLATION CAUGHT BY OPERATOR

**Operator audit**: if limit 75200 filled at default 3x leverage:
- 50k: IM $25,067 / equity $49,357 = **50.8%**
- 200k: IM $100,267 / equity $197,464 = **50.8%**

Both **2× над HyroTrader 25% margin cap**. Notional (1×/4× BTC = $75k/$300k) под 2× initial rule, но margin/equity при 3x leverage пробивает потолок.

**Root cause**: My risk-pct sizing (0.5% account risk / SL distance 250pts = 1 BTC qty) gave correct risk-based size, BUT margin/equity check отсутствовал в decision. Executor's sizing math = correct for risk rule; сhecks against margin rule — отсутствуют.

**Action**: `cancel-limit --symbol BTCUSDT --reason expired` → **ok=true, had_pending=true**. Оба аккаунта cleaned.

**Outcome**: 0 P&L impact (никогда не filled). Сохранение от compliance breach.

**Lesson (codify в lessons-learned.md)**: 
> Before any BTC limit/entry near-market with tight SL, verify `notional / (equity × leverage) ≤ 0.25`. At 3x leverage, qty × price < equity × 0.75 (quick check = equity × 3 × 0.25 = 75% of 3× equity in notional max). For 50k equity → max notional ~$37k при 3x. My $75k notional = 2× over.
> Executor lacks this guard currently — TO-FIX add pre-flight margin check.

**Decision**: FLAT. Heat 0%. Waiting for cleaner setup that respects margin ceiling — smaller qty OR different leverage OR different pair.
